  (=

    (==

  :- dynamic'is-variable'/1.

  'is-variable'(_x1) :-
    eval([==, ['get-metatype', _x1], 'Variable'], _x1).
  (: lazy-or 
    (-> Bool Atom Bool))
  (=

  :- dynamic'lazy-or'/2.

    eval_false(A).

  (=

  (: is-closed 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-closed $x) 
    (if 
      (is-variable $x) False 
      (if 
        (== () $x) True 
        (if 
          (is-expression $x)

  :- dynamic'is-closed'/1.

  'is-closed'(_x5) :-
    (   eval_true(['is-variable', _x5])
    *-> _x5='False'
    ;   (   eval_true([==, [], _x5])
        *-> A='True'
        ;   (   eval_true(['is-expression', _x5])

                  eval(['cdr-atom', _x5], _tail1)

                B=C
            ;   C='True'
            ),
            C=A
        ),
        A=_x5
    ).
